  0 2 2 →= 2 3 3 5 5 4 0 3 3 0 ,
  5 5 1 →= 3 0 5 5 0 0 0 0 4 4 ,
  0 4 0 0 →= 2 3 3 5 2 4 2 3 3 5 ,
  0 1 2 4 1 →= 0 5 0 2 2 2 5 3 4 4 }

After renaming modulo the bijection { 5 ↦ 0, 0 ↦ 1, 4 ↦ 2, 2 ↦ 3, 3 ↦ 4, 1 ↦ 5 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 6-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 1 2 1 2 ⟶ 0 3 4 1 1 2 2 1 0 2 ,
  0 0 5 4 0 0 5 ⟶ 4 0 0 5 2 4 1 4 1 5 ,
  2 1 2 3 1 5 4 ⟶ 2 3 3 0 2 5 1 0 1 0 ,
  3 →= 1 0 1 4 4 3 4 4 1 1 ,
  1 3 3 →= 3 4 4 0 0 2 1 4 4 1 ,
  1 2 1 1 →= 3 4 4 0 3 2 3 4 4 0 }

Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].

  3 →= 1 0 1 4 4 3 4 4 1 1 ,

  1 2 1 1 →= 3 4 4 0 3 2 3 4 4 0 }
